```
assignment-expression
```

* expression
* initializer

```
conditional-expression
         ::= logical-and-expression ( 'OR' logical-and-expression )*
```

```
unary-expression
         ::= primary-expression ( 'LBRACK' expression 'RBRACK' | 'LPAREN' assignment-expression* 'RPAREN' )*
           | unary-operator cast-expression
```

referenced by:

* assignment-expression

```
iteration-statement
```
